# Verba orationis in funere Riarii, per genera et lemmata

Verba sunt **4128**, lemmata **1364**. Sine [LiLa URL](https://lila-erc.eu/) remanent verba **15**, lemmata **13**.

Tabulam fecit XQuery programma [ListLemmataLiLaOcc.xq](scripta/ListLemmataLiLaOcc.xq) ex DB `modr-riar-lemm`, factam per XQuery [createModrRiarLemmataDB.xq](scripta/createModrRiarLemmataDB.xq).

## Lemmata sine LiLa URL

Sine [LiLa URL](https://lila-erc.eu/) remanent verba **15**, lemmata **13**.

+ Bosti, proper noun (LiLa 0)
+ Imola, proper noun (LiLa 0)
+ Maiolus, proper noun (LiLa has maiolus, common noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/63245 )
+ Modrusiensis, adjective (LiLa 0)
+ Perusium (LiLa has perusia, proper noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/18135 )
+ Saona, proper noun (LiLa 0)
+ Symoniacus (LiLa has simonia, common noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/80774 )
+ Ticinium (LiLa has ticinum, proper noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/23667 )
+ Vicheria, proper noun (LiLa has uiceria, common noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/84994)
+ Viterbiensis, adjective (LiLa has uiterbium, proper noun: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/136052 )
+ computum, common noun, neutrum (variant of computus: https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/95420 )
+ floccipendo, verb (written as one word; composite of floccus, noun https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/103468 and pendo 3, verb https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/116474 ); CroALa [2 occurrences in Nikola Modruki](http://solr.ffzg.hr/philo4/croala0/query?report=concordance&method=proxy&q=floccipend.*&start=0&end=0)
+ nudiustertius, adverb (written as one word; there is an adverb nudius https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/113942 and adjective nudiustertianus https://lila-erc.eu/data/id/lemma/113943 ); CroALa [10 occurrences](http://solr.ffzg.hr/philo4/croala0/query?report=concordance&method=proxy&q=nudiustertius&start=0&end=0)
